Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

Two New Chrysler Airflow Cars

— Hua

Spacious and beautiful, famous in the market

According to Mr. Mardi of Mardi Motors, the 1935 Chrysler Airflow has long been famous in the market. Recognizing the increasing need for spacious and luxurious cars, two new car bodies with extended wheelbases have been manufactured to meet the demand.

The first is a refined and stylish seven-seater sedan. It is spacious and comfortable to ride in, providing unexpected pleasure. It can accommodate seven passengers without crowding. The overall trim and paint are extremely beautiful. It has the skills and economy of the Chrysler Airflow, and the seats are wide and comfortable.

The extended wheelbase is sufficient for manufacturing a more beautiful and convenient five-seater touring sedan. Therefore, the latest five-seater Chrysler Airflow touring sedan has been successfully manufactured and is on the market for sale. Its spaciousness is unprecedented for a car of the same type, which is exactly what is needed now. The car has a large trunk, which is part of the entire body. The car's beauty and practicality are thus further enhanced.

The Chrysler Airflow has been known in the market this year as a car with high skill and low cost. All its various features are also available in these two new models with extended wheelbases. Such as the simultaneous silent transmission, the new conical roof spring, the four-wheel hydraulic brake, the all-steel body, and the simplified ventilation system that does not obstruct the line of sight are the most prominent of its characteristics.

On the left is the newly released Chrysler Airflow seven-seater sedan with a long wheelbase of 128 inches.

Dodge Also Releases Two New Car Bodies

According to Mr. Freeman, the general manager of China Motors, Dodge engineers have always been known for manufacturing spacious and comfortable cars. In order to promote its established reputation, two new car bodies have been released. From now on, the various models of the 1935 Dodge cars will be even more beautiful.

The first is a seven-seater Dodge sedan. The second is a five-seater Dodge touring sedan. Both of the above cars use extra-long wheelbases. Other manufacturing is the same as those circulating in the market. The so-called seven-seater sedan is most suitable for those who need extra-large seats. Because it is spacious and can seat seven people, there is absolutely no crowding. Even the two passengers sitting in the passenger seat can enjoy unprecedented comfort. In addition, it offers many additional features that are very popular with passengers.

As for the five-seater Dodge touring sedan, its luxury is no less than that of the seven-seater sedan. It also has a trunk, which is an integral part of the car body. Because its wheelbase is extended, the space in the car has been enlarged. Not only is the legroom for rear passengers more comfortable, but the luggage space has also increased significantly. Therefore, it has truly discovered a new meaning in the comfort of car travel. At the same time, all the engineering features for which Dodge cars are famous this year are also available in these two Dodge cars. Such as independent front suspension, unibody all-steel body, four-wheel hydraulic brakes, new springs, fingertip transmission, and buoyancy engine installation.

Car Electricity Knowledge

— Chen Xing

Every component of a car should be used in the proper way and with the proper procedure. The same is true for electricity. The following are the points related to car electricity, divided into sections.

(1) When turning on the water, turn on the ignition circuit with a key or button. The pointer on the ammeter should point to the "Discharge" side. If the meter pointer remains motionless, there must be something wrong with the ignition system. It needs to be diagnosed and treated.

(2) When lifting or stepping on the starter motor button, it should be firm. Do not loosen or tighten it suddenly. A few seconds is enough. Do not overdo it, as it will damage the battery. In cold weather, the carburetor can be stepped down at the same time. In this way, the motor is easier to shake the engine. After the engine starts, it should be loosened immediately to restore it to its original state.

(3) After the car is driven out, even if the speed reaches 10 to 12 miles per hour, even if the lights are not turned on, the ammeter pointer still does not point to the "Charge" side. The car should be stopped and inspected and repaired.

(4) Use the horn loudly in the wilderness and quietly in the bustling city. It should be followed and must not be mistaken. Do not use it too much when it is not necessary, especially in crowded places.

(5) When driving at night, use high beams in the countryside and low beams in the city. Do not use them upside down or randomly. When meeting a car, the high beam should be adjusted to low beam, or even turned off, so that the other driver's vision is not disturbed by the lights and accidents are avoided.

(6) The electricity charged into the battery by the generator should be increased or decreased according to the needs. If you are driving a long distance during the day, the charging rate can be reduced. Conversely, if you stop many times, the charging rate should be increased. However, the average charging rate should not exceed 10 amps.

(7) To increase or decrease the charging rate of the generator, the generator cover can be removed and the third brush moved. Move it in the direction of rotation to increase the charging rate. Move it in the opposite direction to reduce the charging rate. In winter, when more electricity is used, the third brush should be moved slightly in the direction of rotation to increase the charging rate.

(8) The conductors and brushes of the generator should be polished and cleaned every three months so that the generator can work smoothly.

(9) The battery should be checked every week. If you find that the water level is insufficient, you must immediately fill it with distilled water. But do not add electrolyte. When adding water in winter, it should be done before using the car.

(10) The ampere-hour of the battery and the amount of volts. (For example, the Ford V-shaped eight-cylinder car uses an 80 ampere-hour, 6-volt battery) should be noted when replacing the battery according to the regulations.

(11) When the engine stops working, the ignition circuit must be disconnected immediately. Do not turn on the lights or press the horn, so that the battery does not suffer unexpected losses.

(12) The amount of electricity stored in the battery can be measured with a specific gravity meter. If the specific gravity is between L275 and L300, the power storage is sufficient. If it is L265-L260 density, the stored electricity has been gradually consumed. The method of using pliers handles to connect the electrical terminals horizontally to ignite sparks to determine the amount of electricity stored should be avoided as much as possible.

(13) The vent holes on the plugs of each battery should be paid attention to at all times to prevent them from being blocked by dirt. The outside of the battery should be washed frequently. When it is extremely dirty, it can be washed with ammonia and soda water.

(14) The area around the electrical terminals should be kept clean at all times. If dirt occurs, use a flat fine file to scrape it off and clean it, and then apply Vaseline to minimize corrosion.

(15) If the battery consumes too much water, the charging rate is too high. At this time, the charging rate of the generator should be reduced. If the specific gravity is too low, the electricity supplied by the generator is insufficient. At this time, the charging rate should be increased.

(16) If the vehicle is not used for a long time, the wires installed on the positive and negative terminals of the battery must be loosened. Each battery should also be filled with distilled water. When reinstalling, the grounding (either positive or negative) should follow the original regulations. There must be no mistakes. After reinstalling, the clamp should be locked tightly to prevent the battery from being shaken violently.

(17) In winter, the battery should always be kept with a sufficient amount of electricity. The specific gravity must be at least L250 density. Otherwise, there is a risk of freezing.

(18) The plugs of each battery must be tightened to prevent the electrolyte from spilling out. The electrolyte is acidic. Do not pour it on the car paint and cushions to avoid damage.

(19) The leather wires connecting the spark plugs on the distributor cover are installed according to the firing order of the cylinders. Do not change them arbitrarily.

(20) For new cars, the timing of the spark is mostly self-adjusted. If it is not automatic, when starting the engine, the spark button must be placed in the latest position. When the engine speed increases, the spark button should also be placed in an earlier position.

(20) (1) If the power-off point in the distributor is burned out, causing uneven firing, a file for making clocks or jewelry can be inserted into the contact point, and the two contact surfaces can be pressed flat with your fingers. This is the best method. Avoid grinding with a file whenever possible.

(22) If the specially made tubular leather wire connector on the distributor cover is soaked in oil or water, it can hinder the firing work. Therefore, you must be careful to prevent it. If it is accidentally stained, it should be wiped clean with a dry cloth immediately.

(23) The spark plugs must be inspected frequently. If the magnets are covered with carbon deposits, they must be scraped off with a small knife and washed with gasoline. If the gap is too wide or too narrow, it should be adjusted. The proper gap is about twenty-five thousandths of an inch.

(24) After the car has traveled 10,000 miles, it is best to replace the spark plugs with new ones. Because spark plugs are easy to break, replacing them with new ones can make the engine work smoothly and increase the power produced.

(25) The voltage and candlepower of the bulb must be in accordance with the original regulations. When replacing, you should pay attention. Do not replace them casually.

(26) There are oil holes and oil cups next to the generator and distributor. Every five hundred or one thousand miles, the engine oil should be filled once.

(27) Do not allow the water used to wash the car to soak the wires, the spark plug installation on the cylinder head, and other electrical components, causing leakage and hindering their work.

(28) If the wires and cables are slightly damaged, they must be replaced immediately. Otherwise, wrapping them with tape can also be used temporarily.

(29) You should inspect all wire connectors from time to time to see if they are loose. A Inspect the wires connecting the spark plugs. B Inspect the wires connecting the step-up box. C Inspect the wires connecting the generator and circuit breaker. D Inspect the wires connecting the starter motor and battery. L Wires connected to the dashboard.

(30) If the engine has stopped running and the lights have also been turned off, but the ammeter pointer still points to "Discharge," then you can choose one of the battery's electrical terminals and remove its connection wire. At this time, if the meter pointer goes to "0," there must be a leakage in the electrical system. It should be repaired.

Actual Progress of Zhejiang Province's Recent Highways (Continued)

— Cheng Yuqing

(20) Longyou-Suichang-Songyang Section and Longxi Section: The trunk line of this section starts from Zhongshan in Suichang and ends in Songyang. The branch line starts from Suichang County to Zhongshan and from Longyou to Xikou. The construction of road surface and bridges by conscripted labor in Longyou County has been fully completed.

(21) Tongcun-Xucun and Tongcun-Yancun Roads: These two roads connect to Changshan-Tongcun Road. Starting from Tongcun, one goes to Xucun and the other to Yancun. Both are border defense roads. The construction was done by conscripted labor in Kaihua County. The earth road has been completed.

(22) Connection Lines of Various Highways: 1. Quzhou-Lanxi-Lanshou Connection Line: From Magongzui of Quzhou-Lanxi Road, across the river, along the mountain to near Xixi Market, to connect to Lanshou Road. Constructed by the Highway Bureau. 2. Jinhua Connection Line: Starting from Jinhua Station of Jinhua-Wuyi-Yongkang Road, crossing the Yiwu Port, passing through the city to Jinhua Station of Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. Constructed by Jinhua County raising funds.

(23) Branch Lines to Scenic Areas: 1. Linglong Mountain Branch Line in Lin'an: From Linglong Station of Hangzhou-Huizhou Road to the foot of Linglong Mountain. 2. Fishing Terrace Branch Line: From Zhisha Town of Tonglu-Jiande Road to the foot of Yan Ziling's Fishing Terrace. 3. North Mountain Branch Line: From Jinhua Connection Line to Luodian Village at the foot of North Mountain. 4. Fangyan Branch Line: From Shiya Village of Leqing-Yongkang Road to Yanqian Street at the foot of Fangyan. 5. Xiandu Branch Line: From Huangbi of Yongkang-Jinyun Road to Xiandu. 6. Tiantai Mountain Branch Line: From Tiantai County of Tiantai-Linhai Road to Guoqing Temple. 7. Yandang Mountain Branch Line: From Zixi in Yueqing of Qingguan Road to the foot of Yandang Mountain. The above lines are being actively rushed to completion. All can be completed uniformly before February of the 24th year [of the Republic], in order to facilitate tourists next spring.

Page 26

(24) Jiaxing-Huzhou Road: This road starts from Pingwang in Jiangsu, passes through Nanxun, and ends in Wuxing. It is very important for connecting the Jiaxing-Pinghu and Beijing-Hangzhou Roads. It is currently being rushed to construct first.

(25) Yongjia-Rui'an-Pingyang Road: This road starts from Yongjia, passes through Rui'an and Pingyang, and ends at Qiaomendun on the border of Zhejiang and Fujian. It is one section of the Zhejiang-Fujian trunk line.

(26) Yunhe-Jingning-Taishun Road: This road starts from Yunhe, passes through Jingning, and ends in Taishun. It is currently being rushed to construct.

(27) Longquan-Qingyuan-Ningde Road: This road starts from Longquan, passes through Qingyuan, and ends in Shouning of Fujian Province. It is also one of the border defense highways.

(28) Lishui-Yunhe Road: This road starts from Lishui, passes through Dagangtou, and ends in Yunhe. Part of the earthwork was constructed by conscripted labor from the Lishui and Yunhe County Governments. It started at the end of January in the 22nd year [of the Republic] and was completed in April of the 23rd year. It has now been opened to traffic and is in operation by the Provincial Highway Administration.

(29) Pinghu-Jiaxing Section: This section starts from Pinghu and ends in Jiaxing. It connects the ZhaPu-Pinghu and Jiaxing-Wangjiangjing sections. It was completed in March of the 23rd year [of the Republic]. Later, because the temporary road surface was not very solid, a formal road surface was added. The work was completed again in June, and the entire road was immediately opened to traffic.

(30) Jiande-Chunan Road: This road starts from Baisha Town in Jiande and ends in Chunan County. It was opened in April of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and completed at the end of January of the 23rd year, along with the Jiande-Shouchang Road.

(31) Chunan-Weiping Road: This road starts from Chunan and ends at Weiping on the border of Zhejiang and Anhui. It connects to the Tunxi-Weiping Road in Anhui Province and can directly reach Tunxi. It started in September of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and was completed at the end of June of the 23rd year. The Provincial Highway Administration is preparing to open it to traffic together with the Jiande-Chunan and Jiande-Shouchang Roads.

(32) Fenghua-Xinchang Road: This road starts from Xikou in Fenghua and ends in Yuanmaozhen in Xinchang. It started in November of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and was opened to traffic at the end of June of the 23rd year. However, due to the large scale of the Kangling and Xikou bridges, temporary bridges were used for traffic. The formal bridges are currently being rushed to construct and are expected to be completed at the end of July.

(33) Chunan-Suian Road: This road starts from Chunan and ends in Suian. It started in March of the 22nd year [of the Republic]. The earth road had already been opened to traffic. A simple gravel road surface was laid this year and completed at the end of January.

(34) Highways Operated by Various Counties in the Ningbo Area: 1. Ningbo-Chuanshan Road: From Ningbo, passing through Yuwangling to Chuanshan and the Chaiqiao branch line. Leased and operated by the Ningbo-Chuanshan Company, it was opened to traffic in June. 2. Cixi-Longshan Road: From Cixi, passing through Wenxi to Longshan. Built separately by Cixi and Zhenhai counties. It has now been completed. 3. Wenxi-Camel Bridge Road: From Wenxi to Camel Bridge. 4. Yuyao-Zhouxiang Road: From Yuyao to Zhouxiang. 5. Shengzhen-Hushan Road: From Shengyan in Yuyao to Hushan. All have been constructed and are being prepared for opening to traffic separately.

(35) Guanhaiwei-Zhouxiang Section: This section starts from Guanhaiwei, passes through Hushan, and ends in Zhouxiang. It started in August of the 22nd year [of the Republic]. As of the end of the 22nd year, the roadbed, bridges, and culverts have been completed. It will be opened to traffic in August of this year.

(36) Zhouxiang-Cao'e Section: This section starts from Zhouxiang and ends in Cao'e Baiguan. It started in mid-March of the 22nd year [of the Republic]. As of the end of the 22nd year, it has been largely completed and has been put into operation.

(37) Dongyang-Yongkang Road: This road starts from Leyang and ends in Yongkang. It started at the end of October of the 23rd year [of the Republic] and has been completely completed.

(38) Linhai-Huangyan Road: This road starts from Linhai and ends in Huangyan. It started on April 1st of the 23rd year [of the Republic] and has been fully completed.

(39) Zeguo-Qingjiang Section: This section starts from Zeguo and ends at the Qingjiang ferry in Yueqing. It has been fully completed.

(40) Qingjiang-Guantou Section: This section starts from the Qingjiang ferry in Yueqing and ends in Guantou Town in Yongjia. Together with the Zeguo-Qingjiang section, they are part of the Huangyan-Guangfeng Road, and the project has been completed.

(41) Yongjia-Guantou Section: This section starts from Guantou and ends at Guishan across the river from Yongjia, connecting to the Qingtian-Wenzhou Road. It is 15 kilometers long and has been connected.

(42) Qingtian-Wenzhou Road: This road starts from Qingtian and ends in Yongjia. It started in January of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and has been fully completed.

(43) Lishui-Qingtian Road: This road starts from Lishui and ends in Qingtian. It started in January of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and has been fully completed.

(44) Yunhe-Longquan Road: This road starts from Yunhe and ends in Longquan, connecting to Lishui-Yunhe Road. It started in September of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and has been fully completed.

(45) Fenghua-Ninghai Road: This road starts from Fenghua and ends in Ninghai. It was built in October of the 22nd year [of the Republic] and has now been fully completed.
